    <script>
      (function() {
        window.docLocale = 'en_US';
/**
 **/

const PrimaryCtaService = function() {
};

PrimaryCtaService.prototype.run = function() {
  const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
  if (params.get('hasdomains') === 'true') {
    this.enableHasDomains();
    this.enableHasDomainsResponse();
    return;
  }

  /*  */
  this.activate();
};

PrimaryCtaService.prototype.activate = function() {
  /*  */
  window['dmaHasDomains'] = null;
  const ssHasDomains = sessionStorage.getItem('hasDomains');
  if (ssHasDomains) {
    /*  */
    const hasDomains = (ssHasDomains === 'true');
    window['dmaHasDomains'] = hasDomains;
    if (hasDomains === true) {
      /*  */
      this.enableHasDomains();
    }
    /*  */
    this.enableHasDomainsResponse();
    this.enableHasDomainsResponseFromSessionStorage();
  } else {
    /*  */
    this.updateFromApi();
  }

  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    this.reset();
  }.bind(this), {once: true});
};

PrimaryCtaService.prototype.reset = function() {
  if (window['dmaHasDomains'] === true) {
    this.enableHasDomains();
    this.enableHasDomainsResponse();
  } else if (window['dmaHasDomains'] === false) {
    this.enableHasDomainsResponse();
  } else {
    /*  */
    window['dmaTimeout'] = null;
    window['dmaInterval'] = setInterval(function() {
      if (window['dmaHasDomains'] !== null) {
        if (window['dmaHasDomains'] === true) {
          this.enableHasDomains();
        }
        this.enableHasDomainsResponse();
        clearInterval(window['dmaInterval']);
        clearTimeout(window['dmaTimeout']);
      }
    }.bind(this));
    window['dmaTimeout'] = setTimeout(function() {
      /*  */
      clearInterval(window['dmaInterval']);
      this.enableHasDomainsResponse();
    }.bind(this), 2000);
  }
};

PrimaryCtaService.prototype.enableHasDomains = function() {
  window.setTimeout(function() {
    document.querySelector('body').classList.add('has-domains');
  });
};

PrimaryCtaService.prototype.enableHasDomainsResponse = function() {
  window.setTimeout(function() {
    const bodyEl = document.querySelector('body');
    if (bodyEl.classList.contains('has-domains-response')) {
      return;
    }
    bodyEl.classList.add('has-domains-response');
    if (window['dmaHasDomains'] === false) {
      window.dataLayer.push({'status': '0'});
    } else if (window['dmaHasDomains'] === true) {
      window.dataLayer.push({'status': '1'});
    } else {
      window.dataLayer.push({'status': 'unknown'});
    }

    if (window['cookieConsentUtils'] &&
        cookieConsentUtils.userOptedOut() === true) {
      /*  */
    } else {
      (function(w, d, s, l, i) {
        w[l]=w[l]||[];
        w[l].push({'gtm.start': new Date().getTime(), 'event': 'gtm.js'});
        const f=d.getElementsByTagName(s)[0];
        const j=d.createElement(s);
        const dl=l!='dataLayer'?'&l='+l:'';
        j.async=true;
        j.src='https://www.googletagmanager.com/gtm.js?id='+i+dl;
        f.parentNode.insertBefore(j, f);
      })(window, document, 'script', 'dataLayer', ['GTM-WMNNT4']);

      (function(w, d, s, l, i) {
        w[l]=w[l]||[];
        w[l].push({'gtm.start': new Date().getTime(), 'event': 'gtm.js'});
        const f=d.getElementsByTagName(s)[0];
        const j=d.createElement(s);
        const dl=l!='dataLayer'?'&l='+l:'';
        j.async=true;
        j.src='https://www.googletagmanager.com/gtm.js?id='+i+dl;
        f.parentNode.insertBefore(j, f);
      })(window, document, 'script', 'dataLayer', 'GTM-KQ3J7DH');

      (function(w, d, s, l, i) {
        w[l]=w[l]||[];
        w[l].push({'gtm.start': new Date().getTime(), 'event': 'gtm.js'});
        const f=d.getElementsByTagName(s)[0];
        const j=d.createElement(s);
        const dl=l!='dataLayer'?'&l='+l:'';
        j.async=true;
        j.src='https://www.googletagmanager.com/gtm.js?id='+i+dl;
        f.parentNode.insertBefore(j, f);
      })(window, document, 'script', 'dataLayer', 'GTM-NQ9D55V');
    }
  });
};

PrimaryCtaService.prototype.enableHasDomainsResponseFromSessionStorage = function() {
  window.setTimeout(function() {
    document.querySelector('body').classList.add('has-domains-response-from-sessionstorage');
  });
};

PrimaryCtaService.prototype.updateDefaultButtonLabel = function() {
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    const parents = ['header__menu', 'header__sides__aside'];
    parents.forEach(function(parent) {
      const originalCaption = document.querySelector(`.${parent} .header__user--has-domains`).textContent.trim();
      const notHasDomainsEl = document.querySelector(`.${parent} .header__user--not-has-domains span`);
      notHasDomainsEl.textContent = originalCaption;
    });
  });
};

PrimaryCtaService.prototype.updateFromApi = function() {
  window.dregRelayClient &&
    window.dregRelayClient.getUserData().then(function(value) {
      const hasDomains = value.hasDomains;
      if (hasDomains != null) {
        window['dmaHasDomains'] = hasDomains;
        /*  */
        this.enableHasDomains();
      }
      this.enableHasDomainsResponse();
      sessionStorage.setItem('hasDomains', hasDomains);
    }.bind(this));
};

PrimaryCtaService.prototype.pickRunExperiment = function() {
  /*  */
  if (sessionStorage.getItem('hasDomainsExperimentGroup')) {
    return true;
  }

  /*  */
  sessionStorage.setItem('hasDomainsRunExperiment', 'on');
  return true;

  /*  */
  const shouldRunStorage = sessionStorage.getItem('hasDomainsRunExperiment');
  if (shouldRunStorage != undefined) {
    return shouldRunStorage == 'on';
  }

  /*  */
  const shouldRun = 1.0 >= Math.random(1);
  if (shouldRun) {
    sessionStorage.setItem('hasDomainsRunExperiment', 'on');
    return true;
  }
  sessionStorage.setItem('hasDomainsRunExperiment', 'off');
  return false;
};

PrimaryCtaService.prototype.getExperimentGroup = function() {
  return sessionStorage.getItem('hasDomainsExperimentGroup');
};

PrimaryCtaService.prototype.setExperimentGroup = function(group) {
  sessionStorage.setItem('hasDomainsExperimentGroup', group);
  window.setTimeout(function() {
    document.querySelector('body').classList.add(`has-domains-${group}-group`);
  });
};

PrimaryCtaService.prototype.pickExperimentGroup = function() {
  const isControl = .5 <= Math.random();
  if (isControl) {
    console.log('primary cta: picked control group');
    this.setExperimentGroup('control');
    return 'control';
  }
  console.log('primary cta: picked variation group');
  this.setExperimentGroup('variation');
  return 'variation';
};        window['primaryCta'] = new PrimaryCtaService();
        primaryCta.run();
      })();
